1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
```

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Apache Beam Pipeline Runner Translation Layer

## Your Task

Find all Java source files in apache/beam under runners/core-java/ and runners/core-construction-java/ that translate a Beam pipeline graph into runner-specific execution primitives. Identify: the PipelineTranslator interface, the TransformHierarchy walker, the PTransformOverride mechanism, the ExecutableStagePayload construction, and the BoundedSource/UnboundedSource adapter classes. For each file report its path and key class name.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossorg domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/beam--v2.62.0.

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "SymbolName"}
  ],
  "chain": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}
  ],
  "text": "Narrative explanation of your findings, citing repos and file paths."
}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

Your answer will be scored on:
- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

62-assistanttext-
I've completed the analysis of the Apache Beam codebase and created `/workspace/answer.json` with comprehensive findings about the pipeline translation layer components.

## Summary

The analysis identified **22 key Java source files** and **25 important classes/symbols** across the Apache Beam repository (v2.62.0) that form the pipeline runner translation layer:

### Key Findings:

1. **TransformHierarchy Walker**: The `TransformHierarchy` class with its `Node` inner class serves as the foundational visitor pattern implementation for traversing pipeline transforms.

2. **PTransformOverride Mechanism**: `PTransformOverride` and `PTransformOverrideFactory` classes enable runners to identify and replace specific PTransforms during pipeline execution.

3. **ExecutableStagePayload Construction**: 
   - `ExecutableStage` interface defines stages that can execute in a single SDK harness
   - `ImmutableExecutableStage` provides concrete implementation
   - `ExecutableStageTranslation` handles protobuf serialization

4. **Pipeline Graph Construction**:
   - `PipelineValidator` validates pipeline correctness
   - `GreedyPipelineFuser` and `GreedyStageFuser` fuse stages for optimization
   - `QueryablePipeline` provides query interface over components

5. **Source Adapters**:
   - `BoundedToUnboundedSourceAdapter`: Wraps bounded sources for streaming
   - `BoundedReadFromUnboundedSource`: Wraps unbounded sources for bounded execution
   - Runner-specific adapters (Samza, Spark) for source integration

6. **Core Runner Utilities**: `StateInternals`, `TimerInternals`, and their factory classes in `runners/core-java/` provide the foundation for runner implementations.

All findings are documented in the `/workspace/answer.json` file with complete file paths and class names.

contain the core pipeline translation layer components for runners. The Beam SDK uses a sophisticated architecture for translating user-defined pipelines into runner-specific execution primitives.\\n\\n### Key Components Found:\\n\\n#### 1. **PipelineTranslator Interface and TransformHierarchy Walker**\\n\\nThe `TransformHierarchy` class (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/TransformHierarchy.java) is the foundational component that captures information about a collection of transformations and their associated PCollections. It maintains a tree structure representing the pipeline's transform composition with a `Node` inner class that represents individual transforms in the hierarchy. This serves as the base walker for traversing the pipeline graph.\\n\\nThe TransformHierarchy implements the visitor pattern with its nodes maintaining parent-child relationships and supporting both composite and primitive transforms. It tracks PCollection producers and their inputs, enabling runners to understand the full dependency graph of the pipeline.\\n\\n#### 2. **PTransformOverride Mechanism**\\n\\nTwo complementary classes define the override mechanism:\\n- **PTransformOverride** (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/PTransformOverride.java): Pairs a `PTransformMatcher` with a `PTransformOverrideFactory` to identify and replace matching PTransforms in the pipeline.\\n- **PTransformOverrideFactory** (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/runners/PTransformOverrideFactory.java): Defines the interface for creating replacement PTransforms, including `PTransformReplacement` and `ReplacementOutput` inner classes for managing the replacement logic.\\n\\nThese enable runners to customize how specific transforms are executed. For example, the SplittableParDoViaKeyedWorkItems class (runners/core-java/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/runners/core/SplittableParDoViaKeyedWorkItems.java) uses this mechanism to override splittable ParDo implementations with keyed work item processing.\\n\\n#### 3. **ExecutableStagePayload Construction**\\n\\nThe ExecutableStage interface and related classes handle the construction of executable stages:\\n- **ExecutableStage** (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/ExecutableStage.java): A combination of PTransforms that can be executed within a single SDK harness. It defines the URN \\\"beam:runner:executable_stage:v1\\\" and provides access to components, environment, inputs, side inputs, user states, and output PCollections.\\n- **ImmutableExecutableStage** (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/ImmutableExecutableStage.java): Concrete implementation providing immutable executable stages.\\n- **ExecutableStageTranslation** (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/ExecutableStageTranslation.java): Handles serialization/deserialization of ExecutableStagePayload from protobuf messages.\\n\\n#### 4. **Pipeline Graph Construction and Validation**\\n\\nSeveral classes handle pipeline graph transformation:\\n- **PipelineValidator** (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/PipelineValidator.java): Validates the constructed pipeline for correctness, including validation of executable stages.\\n- **GreedyPipelineFuser** (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/GreedyPipelineFuser.java): Fuses a Pipeline into a collection of ExecutableStages using a greedy algorithm.\\n- **GreedyStageFuser** (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/GreedyStageFuser.java): Fuses stages together to reduce the number of SDK harness invocations.\\n- **FusedPipeline** (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/FusedPipeline.java): Represents a pipeline after fusion into executable stages.\\n- **QueryablePipeline** (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/graph/QueryablePipeline.java): Provides a queryable interface over pipeline components.\\n- **PipelineTranslation** (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/PipelineTranslation.java): High-level translation utilities for converting pipelines to/from runner API format.\\n\\n#### 5. **BoundedSource/UnboundedSource Adapter Classes**\\n\\nThese adapter classes enable flexible source handling:\\n- **BoundedToUnboundedSourceAdapter** (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/util/construction/UnboundedReadFromBoundedSource.java): Wraps a BoundedSource as an UnboundedSource, enabling bounded sources to be used in streaming contexts.\\n- **BoundedReadFromUnboundedSource** (sdks/java/core/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/sdk/io/BoundedReadFromUnboundedSource.java): Wraps an UnboundedSource with specified bounds on records and read time to create a BoundedSource.\\n- **BoundedSourceSystem** (runners/samza/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/runners/samza/adapter/BoundedSourceSystem.java): Samza runner adapter for bounded sources, providing SystemFactory integration.\\n- **UnboundedSourceSystem** (runners/samza/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/runners/samza/adapter/UnboundedSourceSystem.java): Samza runner adapter for unbounded sources with checkpoint support.\\n- **MicrobatchSource** (runners/spark/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/runners/spark/io/MicrobatchSource.java): Spark runner wrapper for UnboundedSource that accommodates Spark's micro-batch oriented nature.\\n\\n#### 6. **Core Runner Internals**\\n\\nThe runners/core-java package contains essential runner implementation utilities:\\n- **StateInternals** (runners/core-java/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/runners/core/StateInternals.java): Interface describing state functionality a runner must provide.\\n- **TimerInternals** (runners/core-java/src/main/java/org/apache/beam/runners/core/TimerInternals.java): Interface for timer management in runners.\\n- **StateInternalsFactory** and **TimerInternalsFactory** (in runners/core-java): Provide key-scoped state and timer internals for keyed operations.\\n\\nThese components work together to enable runners to translate a user-defined Beam pipeline into runner-specific execution primitives while maintaining the semantic correctness of the pipeline computation.\\n\"\n}\n",
